######################
###	New PLC events ###
######################

### hyperappeasement_PLC modifier should be the trigger for the decision to destroy the commonwealth for RUS

### Account for modifiers:
### stanislaw_rule - The inital modifier you get after Stanislaw takes over
### hyperappeasement_PLC - Must be removed by any potop or second sejm collapse
### stanislaw_war_momentum - Must be removed by any potop collapse
### plc_angry_jews - Must be removed by any potop collapse

### Search for Stanislaws Hell in MOD BALTIC for Stanislaw Decisions

####### 222240 Liberum veto

country_event = {
	id = 222240
	title = "EVTNAME222240"
	desc = "EVTDESC222240"
	picture = "sejm" 
	
	trigger = {	exists = yes
	    tag = PLC
		NOT = { has_global_flag = NOBILITY_ARE_GONE }
		constructing_cb_progress = 0.5 #5% progress
		OR = {
			constructing_cb_type = acquire_state
			constructing_cb_type = acquire_state_mid
			constructing_cb_type = acquire_state_late
			constructing_cb_type = conquest
			constructing_cb_type = make_puppet
            constructing_cb_type = release_puppet				
            constructing_cb_type = add_to_sphere
			constructing_cb_type = take_from_sphere
			constructing_cb_type = war_reparations
			constructing_cb_type = liberate_country
			constructing_cb_type = free_peoples
			constructing_cb_type = humiliate
            constructing_cb_type = cut_down_to_size		
			constructing_cb_type = dismantle_forts
			constructing_cb_type = free_allied_cores
		}
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = Liberum_Veto }	
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA222240"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = Liberum_Veto
			duration = 365
		}
		any_owned = {
		   limit = {
		      is_core = PLC
		      owner = { ai = yes }
		   }
		   owner = {
		   add_country_modifier = {
			   name = no_more_war
			   duration = 7
		       } 
		   }
	    }	
	}
}

	}

	}
	
	
	option = { 
	name = "PLC8.A"
	prestige = -5

	limit = { 
		OR = { 
			pop_type = bureaucrats
			pop_type = officers 
			pop_type = soldiers
				}
			}
	ideology = {
			value = conservative
			factor = 0.15
				}
			
	}
	
    capital_scope = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.25 value = liberal } } }	
	
	any_pop = {
			limit = { pop_majority_ideology = liberal }
			random_list = { 50 = { reduce_pop = 0.95 } 50 = { reduce_pop = 0.9 } } 
	    }
    AUS = { country_event = { id = 260005 days = 3 } }
	MUS = { set_country_flag = hapsburg_general }
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = 222438
	title = "PLCN7.T" #BOH/HLR intervention
	desc = "PLCN7.D"	
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	option = { 
	name = "PLCN7.A"
	set_global_flag = PLC_confederacy
	# Remove PLC alliances except with specific tags
	FROM = { country_event = 222439 }
	war = {
		target = PLC
			attacker_goal = {
				casus_belli = custom_treaty_cb
			}
			defender_goal = {
				casus_belli = status_quo
			}

country_event = { 
    id = 2224448
    title = "PLCN24.T"
    desc = "PLCN24.D"

    is_triggered_only = yes
    major = yes

    option = { 
    name = "PLCN24.A"
	   nationalvalue = nv_equality
	   any_country = { 
	      limit = {
	         exists = yes
		     capital = 619
	      }
	      country_event = { id = 260006 days = 1 }
	   }
	   remove_country_modifier = stanislaw_war_momentum
	   clr_country_flag = stanislaw_timelimit
	   set_country_flag = lublin_new
	   set_country_flag = stanislaw_reclamation
	   random_owned = {
	       limit = {
		      owner = {
			     NOT = { has_country_flag = KIE_nobility_pissed }
				 NOT = { has_country_flag = LIT_nobility_pissed }
			  }
		   }
		   owner = {
	          add_accepted_culture = ruthenian
	          add_accepted_culture = galician	
		      add_accepted_culture = lithuanian 
		      add_accepted_culture = belarusian
	          set_country_flag = treaty_hadiach	
			  country_event = { id = 222305 days = 1 }
           }			  
	   }
	   random_owned = {
	       limit = {
		      owner = {
			     has_country_flag = LIT_nobility_pissed
		         NOT = { has_country_flag = KIE_nobility_pissed }
		      }
		   }
		   owner = {
	          add_accepted_culture = ruthenian
	          add_accepted_culture = galician	
           }			  
	   }
	   random_owned = {
	       limit = {
		      owner = {
			     has_country_flag = KIE_nobility_pissed
		         NOT = { has_country_flag = LIT_nobility_pissed }
		      }
		   }
		   owner = {
		      add_accepted_culture = lithuanian 
		      add_accepted_culture = belarusian
		   }
	   }
	   365 = { add_core = PLC }
	   691 = { add_core = PLC }
	   690 = { add_core = PLC }
	   694 = { add_core = PLC }
	   PRU = { all_core = { add_core = PLC } }

	      militancy = -9
	   }
       plurality = -30

country_event = { 
	id = 2224450
	title = "PLCN26.T"
	desc = "PLCN26.D"

    fire_only_once = yes	
	
	trigger = { 
	tag = PLC
	has_country_flag = stanislaw_timelimit
	NOT = { has_country_modifier = stanislaw_war_momentum }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
	days = 31
	}
	
	option = { 
	name = "PLCN26.A"
    remove_country_modifier = plc_angry_jews
	add_country_modifier = {
       name = power_vacuum
	   duration = -1
	}
	add_country_modifier = {
       name = calm_before_storm
	   duration = -1
	}
    country_event = { id = 2224451 days = 31 }	
	}
}

	desc = "PLC28.D"
	picture = "sejm"
	
	major = yes
	
	trigger = { 
	tag = PLC 
	has_country_flag = the_szlactha_purge
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
	months = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
	name = "PLC28.A"
	any_pop = { 
		limit = { 
		pop_type = aristocrats
		}
		reduce_pop = 0.5
		consciousness = 3
		militancy = 3 
	}   
	relation = { who = BOH value = -400 }
	relation = { who = CAE value = -400 }
	relation = { who = GCF value = -400 }
	relation = { who = HLR value = -400 }
	HLR = { diplomatic_influence = { who = HLR value = -400 } }
	any_country = {
	   limit = { 
	     primary_culture = czech
		 NOT = { tag = HLR }
	   }
	   diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -400 }
	}					
	clr_country_flag = the_szlactha_purge
	set_country_flag = the_new_PLC_good_sejm
	}
}

			}

	clr_country_flag = absolute_monarchy_gov
	clr_country_flag = semi_constitutional_monarchy_gov
	clr_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov
	clr_country_flag = presidential_dictatorship_gov
	clr_country_flag = fascist_gov
	clr_country_flag = anarcho_liberal_gov
	clr_country_flag = socialist_republic_gov
	clr_country_flag = fascist_monarchy_gov
	set_country_flag = democracy_gov
	}
	PZN = { all_core = { remove_core = CPL }   }
	PML = { all_core = { remove_core = CPL }   }
	GLM = { all_core = { remove_core = CPL }   }	
	KRA = { all_core = { remove_core = CPL }   }
    }

# The Collapse of the Grand Duchy

country_event = { 
	id = 222302
	title = "LITPRU2.T"
	desc = "LITPRU2.D"
    picture = "vilnus"
	
	major = yes

	trigger = {
    exists = yes
	tag = LIT
    war = no
	OR = {
	   government = absolute_monarchy
	   government = prussian_constitutionalism
	   government = hms_government
    }
    NOT = { vassal_of = PLC }
    NOT = { substate_of = PLC }	
	NOT = { has_global_flag = WAIT_LIT }
	NOT = {
	   OR = {
	      is_secondary_power = yes
		  is_greater_power = yes
		  BLR = { all_core = { owned_by = THIS } }
	   }
	}   	  
    has_global_flag = INDIE_LIT	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
	months = 500 
	modifier = { 
	   factor = 0.4 
	   year = 1870
	}
	modifier = { 
	   factor = 0.2
	   year = 1900
	}
	modifier = { 
	   factor = 0.9 
	   RUS = { exists = yes }
    }
	modifier = { 
	   factor = 0.9
	   RUS = { is_greater_power = yes }
	}
	modifier = { 
	   factor = 0.9 
	   LAT = { exists = yes }
    }
	modifier = { 
	   factor = 0.01
	   SAM = { exists = yes }
    }
	modifier = { 
	   factor = 0.01 
	   NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_core = SAM } }
    }
	}

	option = { 
	name = "LITPRU2.A"
	clr_global_flag = INDIE_LIT	
	set_global_flag = LIT_DEAD
	remove_accepted_culture = lithuanian
	remove_accepted_culture = ashkenazi
	clr_country_flag = lithuania_problem
	SAM = { all_core = { remove_core = LIT } }
	LIT = { all_core = { add_core = BLR } }
	BLR = { all_core = { remove_core = LIT } }
	RUS_360 = { add_core = BLR }
	any_owned = { 
	  limit = { 
	  is_core = SAM
	  NOT = { region = RUS_360 }
	  }
	  secede_province = SAM
    }
	any_country = {
	   limit = {
	   tag = BLR
	   exists = yes
	   }
	   inherit = THIS
	}
    change_tag = BLR
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = 222324
	title = "LITPRU24.T"
	desc = "LITPRU24.D"
    picture = "vilnus"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
	name = "LITPRU24.A"
	any_owned = { remove_core = POL }
	clr_global_flag = WAIT_LIT
	prestige_factor = -0.90
	clr_country_flag = army_reform_banned	
	clr_global_flag = INDIE_LIT
	set_global_flag = LIT_DEAD
	SAM = { all_core = { remove_core = LIT } }
	LIT = { all_core = { add_core = BLR } }
	BLR = { all_core = { remove_core = LIT } }
	government = presidential_dictatorship
	ruling_party_ideology = conservative
	political_reform = none_voting
	political_reform = party_appointed
	political_reform = no_meeting
	political_reform = state_press
	political_reform = state_controlled
	political_reform = underground_parties
	political_reform = closed_borders
	political_reform = mandatory_service
	political_reform = primary_culture_only
	clr_country_flag = tory_election_win
	clr_country_flag = socialist_election_win
	clr_country_flag = liberal_election_win
	clr_country_flag = communist_election_win
	clr_country_flag = fascist_election_win
	clr_country_flag = reactionary_election_win
	clr_country_flag = anarcho_liberal_election_win
	clr_country_flag = social_liberal_election_win
	clr_country_flag = market_liberal_election_win		
		clr_country_flag = paternal_election_win
	clr_country_flag = theocratic_government
	clr_country_flag = merchantrepublic_gov
	clr_country_flag = communist_gov
	clr_country_flag = absolute_monarchy_gov
	clr_country_flag = semi_constitutional_monarchy_gov
	clr_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov
	clr_country_flag = parliamentary_republic_gov
	clr_country_flag = democracy_gov
	set_country_flag = presidential_dictatorship_gov
	clr_country_flag = fascist_gov
	clr_country_flag = anarcho_liberal_gov
	clr_country_flag = socialist_republic_gov
	clr_country_flag = fascist_monarchy_gov
    add_country_modifier = {
			name = the_last_stand_PLC
			duration = 720
	}
	add_country_modifier = {
				name = taiping_draft
				duration = 720
	}
	any_owned = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_building = fort }
			is_core = BLR
		}
		fort = 3
	}
	RUS_360 = { add_core = BLR }
    RUS_718 = { add_core = RUG }
    RUS_360 = { add_core = RUG }
	936 = { add_core = RUG }
	937 = { add_core = RUG }
    961 = {
        limit = {
           is_core = RUS
        }
	    remove_core = RUG
	}
	change_tag = BLR
	any_owned = { 
	   limit = {
	      is_core = SAM
	      NOT = { region = RUS_360 }
		  NOT = { province_id = 936 }
	   }
	   secede_province = SCA
	}
	any_owned = { 
	   limit = {
	      is_core = BLR
	      NOT = { region = RUS_360 }
		  NOT = { province_id = 936 }
	   }
	   secede_province = RUS
	}
	relation = { who = RUS value = -400 }
	diplomatic_influence = { who = RUS value = -400 }	
	leave_alliance = RUS
	relation = { who = SCA value = -400 }
	diplomatic_influence = { who = SCA value = -400 }	
	leave_alliance = SCA
	RUS = { country_event = { id = 222326 days = 1 } }
	SCA = { country_event = { id = 222326 days = 1 } }	
	}
}
